 If they are, then they made their decision
 darasal cheef justise keem joseph or justise wike bisht kii bench ne faisale se pehle kaha ki wo centre sarkaar kii karrwai se aahat hai
 Chief Justice said that the central government should be fair in the matter of President's rule in Uttarakhand but it is behaving like a private party
 ham aahat hai ki centre sarkaar aisa vyavhaar kar rahi he
 How can you think of playing such a game with the court
 cheef justise ne ye bhi kaha ki agar centre sarkaar raashtrapati shashan khatm kar sarkaar banane kii koshish karti he to ye nyaay kaa uphaas hoga
 The Congress government in Delhi sacked SR Bommai's government in Karnataka
 es aar bommai agar supreme court na gaye hote to aaj yah faisla congress ke kaam nahin aata
 This is the beautiful justice of history
 uttarakhand main dance karte congress ke kaaryakarta jab thak kar baithenge to sochenge ki raajnneeti main paramparaayen kaayam karne kii javabdehi bhi dalon ko nibhaani padati he
 That is why Abhishek Manu Singhvi has said that Congress is proud of Indian democracy and judiciary
 vaaki garv he yaa ateet ke gunahon ko lekar afsos bhi
 So far, President's rule has been imposed in India more than 100 times
 har baar kii paristhitiyaan alag rahi hai magar zyadatar baar iskaa raajnneetik durupyog aisa hua he ki sabase pehle shaq hi hota he
 The Congress has said that it will demand a debate on it in the Rajya Sabha
 bijepi ne kaha he ki use jhatka nahin laga he
 Minister of State for Home Kiran Rijiju has said that it is not an embarrassment for us
 unhone congress par hi sanvaidhanik sankat kii zimmedaari daal di
 Rijiju has said that imposition of President's rule was not a mistake of the Central Government
 kailash vijayawargeey ne kaha ki pichley teen din se hoicourt ke bench kii jo tippaniyan aa rahi thim hamen isi tarah ke faisle kii ummid thi
 The comments 29 april ko bahumat pareekshan ke dauraan sabit ho jayega ki kya harish ravat kii sarkaar alpamat main he? jin 9 vidhayakon ne paala badla tha unke bare main faisla nahin aayaa he
 It will be heard on 23 April
 29 april ko harish ravat ko bahumat sabit karnaa he
 It may be difficult for Rawat if the membership of 9 mlas is restored
 sawaal he ki hoicourt ke is faisle ke baad kya ab bhi bijepi kah sakati he ki raashtrapati shashan lagu karnaa galati nahin thi
 a decision has been taken in this case twice in Uttarakhand
 1993 main pakistan main nawaz shareef ko vahaan kii supreme court ne phir se behaal kar diya tha
 Which was dismissed by President Ghulam Isaac Khan
 donon mulkon main wo pehali sarkaar thi jo raashtrapati ke dwaara barkhaastagi ke baad behaal hui thi
 After the decision, a minister of Nawaz Sharif said that neither God nor Visam was found, neither lived nor lived here
 1994 ke es aar bommai faisle main nawaz sharif sarkaar kii bahaali kaa bhi udhaaharan diya gaya he
 President KR Narayanan returned the Union Cabinet's recommendation to impose President's rule twice but the then Central Government did not send the proposal to the President again
 kya raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ko aisa karnaa chahie tha
 In the 80s, the Supreme Court said in the case of PM Kumar v
 Municipal Corporation of Delhi that our High Court is indeed a High Court
 yani hamaari hoicourt bahut acchhee he
 Has Uttarakhand proved this by repeating it today
 aam taur par duusari sarkaar banane ke baad raashtrapati shashan ke maamle main faisle aate rahe hai
 The decision came after the formation of a new government in the SR Bommai case of Karnataka as well
 1989 main centre kii congress sarkaar ne karnataka ke es aar bommai kii sarkaar barkhaast kar di thi
 He was not given a chance to prove his majority in the assembly
 bommai sahab hoicourt main cese haar gaye or phir supreme court gaye
 After several years of hearing in the Supreme Court, the decision came by then his government had gone
 isiilie uttarakhand hoicourt kaa faisla nazir banegaa kyonki usee sarkaar ke rahete faisla aayaa he
 For the first time, the verdict of the SR Bommai case has got a dent
 aam taur par iskaa zikr academik charchaaon main hi hota tha, lekin pehali baar yah hoicourt main faisla aayaa he or puraani sarkaar ko bahumat sabit karne kaa mauka mila he
 This year on 26 January, President's rule was imposed in Arunachal Pradesh, which Congress has challenged in the Supreme Court
 is maamle kii samvidhan peeth main sunwaayee chalati rahi or udhar arunachal main sarkaar banane kii koshishen
 a new government has been formed in Arunachal
 yahaan supreme court main sunwaayee puri ho chuki he lekin faisla aana baaki he
 The decision of the Uttarakhand High Court will therefore be considered bold
 oktober, 2005 main bihar main raashtrapati shashan lagane ke maamle main supreme court kii paanch-sadasyeey bench ne kaha tha ki bihar vidhansabha ko bhang karne kaa raashtrapati kaa aadesh asanvaidhanik tha
 By the time this decision came, the election process had started
 is kaaran supreme court ne dakhal dene se inkaar kar diya tha
 Then Nitish Kumar had said that Prime Minister Manmohan Singh should resign and Bihar Governor Buta Singh should be recalled
 nitish kumaar ne kaha tha ki ham is faisle ko janata ke bich le jaayenge or usase insaaf maangenge
 According to PTI, on October 7, 2005, Arun Jaitley, while speaking to reporters, said that the court has made very strong remarks against the central government
 yahi nahin jab ambedkar jayanti se pehle 26 november ko samvidhan diwas manaane kaa faisla hua to sansad ke donon sadanon main unke yogadan par gambhir charchaa hui
 Taking part in this discussion, Finance Minister Jaitley assured the House in the Rajya Sabha on November 27, 2015 that the apprehension of the use of Article 356 in the States was over
 is aashwaasan ke thik teen maheene baad vahi arun jetali uttarakhand main raashtrapati shashan lagaae jane ko lekar blog likhte hai to uski pehali line ye he, samvidhan kii dhara 356 tab lagu kii jaati he jab raashtrapati is baat se santusht ho jaaen ki kisi rajya main samvidhan ke anusaar shashan nahin kiya ja saktaa or yah vishwaas karne ke paryaapt aadhaar hai
 It is obvious that the basis of satisfaction of the President must have come in the first line because Jaitley may have found this the strongest side, the same argument was given by the lawyer of the Central Government in the High Court but the Uttarakhand High Court has also commented on the President
 Will be considered as an adventure in history
 hoicourt ne kaha ki log galat faisale le sakate hai chaahe ve raashtrapati hon yaa jaj
 This is not the decision of a king who cannot have a judicial review
 centre ke pairokaar kehete rahe ki raashtrapati ne tamaam dastavezon ke aadhaar par apni raajnneetik samajhadaari se faisla liya he
 The High Court said that the decision of the President is not the decision of any king which cannot be reviewed
 uttarakhand hoicourt ke cheef justise ke em joseph or justise wike bisht kii bench ne pehle apana faisalaa reserve rakhane kaa nirnay liya tha lekin jab centre sarkaar ke vakil ye aashwaasan dene ko taiyaar nahin hue ki faisale se pehle raashtrapati shashan hataakar nai sarkaar banane kii koshishen nahin hongi, to unhone apana faisalaa sunaaya
 Actually, the bench of Chief Justice KM Joseph and Justice VK Bisht said before the decision that they are hurt by the action of the central government
 cheef justise ne kaha ki uttarakhand main raashtrapati shashan ke maamle main centre sarkaar ko nishpaksh hona chahie lekin wo privet party jaisaa vyavhaar kar rahi he
 We are hurt that the Central Government is behaving like this
 aap court ke saath aisa khel khilne kii kaise soch sakate hai
 Chief Justice also said that if the Central Government tries to form a government by ending President's rule, then it will be a ridicule of justice
 dilli main baithi congress kii sarkaar ne karnataka ke es aar bommai kii sarkaar barkhaast kii thi
 If SR Bommai had not gone to the Supreme Court, this decision would not have worked for the Congress today
 ye itihaas kaa kuubasurat nyaay he
 When the Congress workers in Uttarakhand dance and sit tired, they will think that the parties have to bear the responsibility of maintaining traditions in politics
 isiilie abhishek manu singhvi ne kaha he ki congress ko bhartiya loktantr or nyaaypalika par garv he
 Really proud or sorry about the sins of the past
 bharat main ab tak 100 se bhi zyada baar raashtrapati shashan lag chukaa he

 congress ne kaha he wo rajya sabha main is par bahes kii maang karegi
 BJP has said that it has not suffered a setback
 grih rajya mantri kiran rigiju ne kaha he ki hamaare liye sharmindagi kii baat nahin he
 He put the responsibility of the constitutional crisis on the Congress itself
 rigiju ne kaha he ki raashtrapati shashan lagaana centre sarkaar kii galati nahin thi
 Kailash Vijayvargiya said that we were expecting a similar decision from the High Court bench which had been coming for the last three days
 tippaniyan During the majority test on April 29, it will be proved whether Harish Rawat's government is in a minority? No decision has been taken on the 9 mlas who were changed
 23 april ko isaki sunwaayee hogi
 On April 29, Harish Rawat has to prove his majority
 agar 9 vidhayakon kii sadsyta behaal ho gai to ravat ke liye mushkil ho sakati he
 The question is that after this decision of the High Court, can the BJP still say that it was not a mistake to impose President's rule
 uttarakhand main do baar is maamle main faisla aayaa he
 Nawaz Sharif was reinstated in Pakistan by the Supreme Court in 1993
 jise raashtrapati ghulaam ishakhaan ne barkhaast kar diya tha
 It was the first government in both countries that was reinstated after the president's dismissal
 faisale ke baad nawaz sharif ke ek mantri ne kaha tha ki na khuda hi mila na visaale sanam, na idhar ke rahe na udhar ke rahe
 The SR Bommai judgment of 1994 also gives an example of the restoration of the Nawaz Sharif government
 raashtrapati ke aar narayanan ne raashtrapati shashan lagane kii kendriya mantrimandal kii sifaarish do baar baar lautaa di lekin tab kii centre sarkaar ne dobaaraa prastaav raashtrapati ke paas nahin bheja tha
 Should President Pranab Mukherjee have done so

 That is, our High Court is very good
 kya aaj uttarakhand ne ise doharaa kar sabit kiya he
 In October 2005, in the case of imposition of President's rule in Bihar, a five-member bench of the Supreme Court stated that the President's order to dissolve the Bihar Legislative Assembly was unconstitutional
 jab tak yah faisla aayaa tab tak chunaav kii prakriya shuru ho chuki thi
 For this reason the Supreme Court refused to interfere
 tab nitish kumaar ne kaha tha ki pradhanmantri manmohan singh ko istipha dena chahie or bihar ke rajyapal bootaa singh ko waapas bulaayaa janaa chahie
 Nitish Kumar had said that we will take this decision among the public and demand justice from him
 pitiai ke anusaar 7 aktubar 2005 ko arun jetali ne patrakaron se baat karte hue kaha tha ki adaalat ne centre sarkaar ke kilaaf behad sakht tippanee kii he
 Not only this, when it was decided to celebrate Constitution Day on 26 November before Ambedkar Jayanti, his contribution was discussed in both the houses of Parliament
 is charchaa main bhaag lete hue 27 november ko 2015 ko rajya sabha main vitt mantri jetali ne sadan ko aashwast kiya tha ki rajyon main anuchhed 356 ke beza istemaal kii ashankaayen samaapt ho chuki hai
 Just three months after this assurance, Arun Jaitley writes a blog about the imposition of President's rule in Uttarakhand, then its first line is this, Article 356 of the Constitution is implemented when the President is satisfied that the constitution in a state Cannot be ruled according to and that there are sufficient grounds to believe it
 zaahir he raashtrapati kii santushti ko aadhaar banane kii baat pehali pankti main isliye ai hogi kyonki jetali ko yah sabase majboot paksh laga hoga, yahi tark centre sarkaar ke vakil ne bhi hoicourt main diya lekin uttarakhand hoicourt ne raashtrapati par bhi jo tippanee kii he wo nyaaypalika ke itihaas main adarpurvak saahasik maani jaaegi
